<div id="review_1094092051" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1094092051" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1094092051?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Mia Sheridan Fans, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1094092051" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17587685241858909509"><b>5 Seriously Meaningful Stars<br/>* * * * * <i> Spoiler Free</i><br/>People who don't read Romance may not have an understanding of how big a category it is...they may do a knee jerk reaction to ... oh, you read that...and dismiss all of the work as trivial saying, "Those books could never be as important as the other works of fiction out there"...or "They are just a bunch of plot points to get to hot scenes or grunting alphas "... <br/><br/>I have been reading Romance now for more than a few years. The quality and variety</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17587685241858909509" style="display:none"><b>5 Seriously Meaningful Stars<br>* * * * * <i> Spoiler Free</i><br>People who don't read Romance may not have an understanding of how big a category it is...they may do a knee jerk reaction to ... oh, you read that...and dismiss all of the work as trivial saying, "Those books could never be as important as the other works of fiction out there"...or "They are just a bunch of plot points to get to hot scenes or grunting alphas "... <br><br>I have been reading Romance now for more than a few years. The quality and variety is vast; but for the most part, all I have read has had crafting, intention and skill. <br><br>Mia Sheridan is an author who can hold her own and then some with any other author of any genre in my book. </b>Her ability to be consistently original in a way where it is almost impossible, astounds. She created a series based on the Love Signs and each one I have read has been a complete journey of discovery for the characters as well as this reader.<br> <br>In Becoming Calder, Ms. Sheridan has taken elements of off the grid cults with a strong nod to child abduction stories and mixed them with a love story so encompassing, it will take your breath away.<br><br>She immerses us; indoctrinates through the eyes of Calder... a true believer from birth. He is goodness personified. A young boy who knows of no other life but on the grounds of Arcadia...he lives in a small two room cabin with his parents and sister; no electricity, running water, plumbing or modern conveniences...at least not for the workers. The council members, as well as the Father, had all the normal things you and I take for granted. It was justified by the Father explaining all were equal in the eyes of the Gods... and it was the gift of the workers to "know" their place and give their work to the council and him.<br><br>Calder is happy being productive, honoring his parents and loving his sister, Maya. She is special to him... so full of love... as a Downs Syndrome child... she is free with her heart. He is a smart, giving being and is devoted to his family...yet he does have a bit of rebel strength in him. His best friend, Xander, has it too... and together they break rules, like sneaking sugar cubes... and dream of the butterscotch candies from the main house. This willful streak takes Calder at 10 to rush and set himself in a spot so he can see the "special one" Father Hector has brought back. For she is to be the "Savior" and all have been waiting for her.<br><br>She is Eden; a petite, blond little girl dressed up in a lace bridal gown being lead down an aisle. As she reaches the main podium, her eyes look out and the two see each other... she sees a young strong face with a sweet smile and caring heart... he is struck by her beauty with quivering lips and look of concern.. They have connected... and he is overcome with the desire to make her feel safe and sure... to rush to her and hold her hand... <br><br>But they are not to be...for she is to marry the Father when she turns 18. It is destined... and he is a worker not a high level council family member.<br><br>These children grow... their attachment to each other grows from a distance until one day Eden risks everything and tries to play with the worker kids. She ventures out to their game and is shunned by one as he says she is not one of them... they are weeds and she is a flower.Calder steps forward; he says yes, she is a flower... but she is like the Morning Glory... beautiful as a flower but strong as a weed...This will be the turning point for them... because Calder has seen the true Eden... her strength, beauty and willingness to endure.<br><br>This book is more than a take off of Romeo and Juliet... lovers who should remain apart but don't... this encompasses, for me so much more. Yes, this was a beautiful heartbreaking love story.<br>There were moments which made me stop because my heart hurt and then was so full I couldn't breathe...There was beauty described and experienced here; to read what was put of the page was a gift. We follow their journey... their discovery of their need and love of one another... their strength to make this impossibility become a reality against all odds.<br><br>The development of this is believable... there is no rush... it is innocent, pure and profound. These two characters become people who grow together, share and discover their meaning of life and cling to the belief of goodness under such oppressing conditions.<br><br>There was another overwhelming part to this story; one of evil and manipulation. To see how it was explained; how it was cloaked in religion and purity was abhorrent to me. Unfortunately, I remember watching live the coverage of Jamestown from its first discovery to its horrifying end.<br><br>This book is partnered with <b>Finding Eden.</b> After sitting for over 5 hours and reading this straight through, I was fortunate to have the book ready to go. It did not disappoint in any way. <br><br>Please read these books...it is my sincere belief, this journey will have an impact on you personally. I know it did me. <br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22847812.Finding_Eden" title="Finding Eden by Mia Sheridan" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1406853564s/22847812.jpg" alt="Finding Eden by Mia Sheridan" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Finding Eden<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1094185071">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></b><br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img alt=" photo banner_zpsb3ab83a0.jpg" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407612151i/10746470._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div></span>

<div id="review_1822001838" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1822001838" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1822001838?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23196814-becoming-calder">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-p-z">authors-p-z</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1822001838" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12230865552649938868">Becoming Calder is the 1st book in a 2-book series and tells the story two people whose courage, goodness and love triumphs over evil. <blockquote>
  <b>“I had dreams as well. In that moment, right there and then, I admitted to myself that I longed for more for my life and maybe those dreams were beautiful too. Brave. I had always pushed that desire away, ashamed of it, thinking it sinful, selfish.<br/>But maybe, just maybe, my own dreams weren’t as sinful as I’d always thought them to be…somehow.” </b>
</blockquote>Mia Sheridan ha</span>
  <span id="freeText12230865552649938868" style="display:none">Becoming Calder is the 1st book in a 2-book series and tells the story two people whose courage, goodness and love triumphs over evil. <blockquote>
  <b>“I had dreams as well. In that moment, right there and then, I admitted to myself that I longed for more for my life and maybe those dreams were beautiful too. Brave. I had always pushed that desire away, ashamed of it, thinking it sinful, selfish.<br>But maybe, just maybe, my own dreams weren’t as sinful as I’d always thought them to be…somehow.” </b>
</blockquote>Mia Sheridan has written an extraordinary tale of conquering your fears despite the many obstacles that face you and how truth and goodness always find the light in your life.<blockquote>
  <b>“But of course, life never worked that way. You had to live every minute of the hard part in order to get to the good.” </b>
</blockquote>This book begins with the two protagonists, Calder and Eden first meeting as children when she's brought to the religious community that he has lived since he can remember, as their leader's future wife.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480172433i/21281674.jpg" alt=" photo kijuu_zpsi1a9vtqr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Under the most pervasive and sinister circumstances, a bond of friendship and love blooms between these two engaging characters. Their love story takes place over several years as the two face the hardships and struggles that come with their finding happiness together. Their story touched me deeply....they have this innocence...and at the same time something so powerful, deep and consuming that is so poignant and so touching.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480172433i/21281675.jpg" alt=" photo 46756498-256-k7104_zps8pvsicr1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>The characters development is very well done. They're memorable, they drive the story and transport you into their lives. <br><br>I found Calder and interesting character. He questions what he has believed in most of his life - what if there something else, something more.......<blockquote> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480172433i/21281676.jpg" alt=" photo 5120Eros20Liber20-20Google20Chrome_zps6iwyvqjz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote>Eden just pulled me in from the first moment she's introduced......... <blockquote>
  <b>In this place, there is a girl with the face of an angel and a heart full of courage. To her family, she is the vision of obedient perfection. But she dares to want that which she has been told can never be hers.</b>
</blockquote>There's something magical and beautiful about her that draws you in.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480172433i/21281677.jpg" alt=" photo da9511e4f540699fddde02a77adee393_zps7rnqc0ep.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Another character I liked, was Xander, Calder's best friend. They have an incredible bond and I am interested to finding out how their friendship develops in the next book.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480172433i/21281678.jpg" alt=" photo holdinghands_zpsh9d4tupa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>The author's depiction of the community's daily life is filled with a sense of evil.....you can feel it ....the menace that permeates around the members who may question the cult leaders words is pretty scary and chilling.<br><br>This book ends in a huge cliff-hanger and Calder and Eden's story continues with Finding Eden, the next book.<br><br>A beautifully written and captivating story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12230865552649938868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review3328948822">

Had I known it was about religious cults there would no way I would have willingly picked this up.<br/><br/>The love story between Calder and Eden was quite sweet friendship to young lovers. <div id="review_1034987174" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1034987174" />
    <a title="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books"><img alt="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1437129491p2/28806659.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1034987174?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" href="/user/show/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books">Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23196814-becoming-calder">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=part-of-series">part-of-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=swoon-worthy">swoon-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=3-point-five-stars">3-point-five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=favorite-couple">favorite-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=in-the-minority">in-the-minority</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=stoppp-it-hurts">stoppp-it-hurts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=fluffy-romance">fluffy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1034987174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11128741636158460466"><b>"3.5 spring stars"</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420213958i/13190660._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Becoming Calder was beautiful story of hope, dreams, friendship and innocent young love. Mia Sheridan has a unique way of shaping up the characters we could relate to, cherishing their growing love and living every moment of this mesmerizing romance. The author never disappoints in the department of romance, one of the my favorite scene was when Calder and Eden made love for the first time under the full moon, by their hidden spring, surrounded by candlelight was so MAGICAL!!!</span>
  <span id="freeText11128741636158460466" style="display:none"><b>"3.5 spring stars"</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420213958i/13190660._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Becoming Calder was beautiful story of hope, dreams, friendship and innocent young love. Mia Sheridan has a unique way of shaping up the characters we could relate to, cherishing their growing love and living every moment of this mesmerizing romance. The author never disappoints in the department of romance, one of the my favorite scene was when Calder and Eden made love for the first time under the full moon, by their hidden spring, surrounded by candlelight was so MAGICAL!!! I was so overwhelmed by their innocence and purity that I just didn’t want this spell to ever end.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“As long as we’re both under the same moon, <br>we’ll always find a way to each other.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>I love Eden and Calder so so much! You don’t get to see powerful heart gripping young romance, where they are drawn to each other against all the odds. Despite being forbidden they create their very own paradise, their hidden spring where they fell in love.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "I’ll always consider it to be the place <br>where my life began.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><b>Rating Clarification</b>: <i>"It's not you, it's me"</i> <br>My rating doesn’t mean I didn’t enjoy this book , it’s just that it didn’t amaze me. Growing up watching Indian movies, this subject matter wasn’t something new to me. The religious cult, brainwashing the community, restricting them against modern way of living and forbidden love was something which has been told and retold in movies ages back. Worst kind of punishment were given to the young lovers who were caught and let me tell you it never ended well! So this story didn’t surprise me at all though the ending was way too intense it was not as bad as I expected it to be. <br><br><b>I had few issues with the plot</b>-#1-<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ how did Eden get pregnant when Calder didn’t come inside her or did I miss something in my sex education class?!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> #2- ok! Let’s say the cult leader Hector made everyone believe there was going to be a major flood killing everyone! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ was the flood coincidence or was Hector right all along? Or did he foresee it? And most important question how was Eden the lone survivor of this flood???? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Overall I liked it but I didn’t love it as such, Archer’s voice still remains my favorite from this author and I’m definitely looking forward to read her future books because let’s face it nobody writes sweet YA/NA romance like Mia. Speaking of her books sorry to keep this review short but I’m dying to read Finding Eden to see how their story ends. <br><br><i>Photo courtesy: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/pattiohara1964/becoming-calderfinding-eden-by-mia-sheridan/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11128741636158460466" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=2020">2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1080517368" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2898700361550895010">This is Book 1 of 2, must be read in order!<br/><br/>What can I say, this is Mia Sheridan and she’s simply one of the best authors there is. Her stories are just full of beauty. They are complex and clever and they keep you hooked the entire time. This duet is no exception, it’s absolutely perfect. I can’t ever recommend her books enough. She’s the best, and Eden and Calder’s story will stay in your heart fore</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=captivity">captivity</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1050953192" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer294582711355240661"><b>3 Powerful Stars</b><br/><br/>I don't know....I don't know...I liked this. <br/><br/>Mia Sheridan is an amazing storyteller and I really enjoy her books. <i>Becoming Calder</i> was a very interesting story and Eden and Calder were really sweet characters. <br/><br/>I think my only issue with this story is that I was pretty much pissed off the entire time, in a very uncomfortable way. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[I hate seeing truly innocent characters who are ignorant of the contemporary word by no fault of their own being taken advantage of in this</span></span>
  <span id="freeText294582711355240661" style="display:none"><b>3 Powerful Stars</b><br><br>I don't know....I don't know...I liked this. <br><br>Mia Sheridan is an amazing storyteller and I really enjoy her books. <i>Becoming Calder</i> was a very interesting story and Eden and Calder were really sweet characters. <br><br>I think my only issue with this story is that I was pretty much pissed off the entire time, in a very uncomfortable way. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I hate seeing truly innocent characters who are ignorant of the contemporary word by no fault of their own being taken advantage of in this manner. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> While I get that a good story - which this absolutely was! - is supposed to make you <i>feel</i> and all that jazz, for me my anger and frustration in the face of such happenings virtually overtakes my enjoyment of the story. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412957159ra/11447814.gif" width="498" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>love</b> reading books that make you sit on the edge of your seat and make you feel all angsty, but feeling angry to the point where I'm almost sick to my stomach for the duration is just not enjoyable for me. <br><br>I would <b>definitely, absolutely</b> recommend this book (as well as pretty much anything written by this author) to anyone who is looking for a powerful, well written YA-style novel. Like I said, the characters are well fleshed out and the romance here is a sweet one. <br><br>This review and rating simply reflect <i>my</i> personal reading experience, however, and I would not want to discourage anyone from reading this beautiful story. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1060357743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17283254244475306522">3.5-4 I've Always Been Yours Stars!<br/>(BR with Patty & Dee)<br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/8571a988-36ec-4445-bfcd-5bd128ef2905.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/b1bde185-4dc6-40bc-944d-0e86a08b53d0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Calder Raynes lives with his family at a 400 acre compound in Arizona called Acadia. The whole community is led by a cult leader named Hector Bias. He takes advantage of these people who are desperate to belong, and tells them lies about the end of the world, & the gods. There are the council members at Acadia who have all the riches & modern day luxuries, & then there are the workers who have nothing, and live in very poor conditio</span>
  <span id="freeText17283254244475306522" style="display:none">3.5-4 I've Always Been Yours Stars!<br>(BR with Patty &amp; Dee)<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/8571a988-36ec-4445-bfcd-5bd128ef2905.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418502165i/12812045._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8571a988-36ec-4445-bfcd-5bd128ef2905.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/b1bde185-4dc6-40bc-944d-0e86a08b53d0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418505163i/12812566.jpg" alt=" photo b1bde185-4dc6-40bc-944d-0e86a08b53d0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Calder Raynes lives with his family at a 400 acre compound in Arizona called Acadia. The whole community is led by a cult leader named Hector Bias. He takes advantage of these people who are desperate to belong, and tells them lies about the end of the world, &amp; the gods. There are the council members at Acadia who have all the riches &amp; modern day luxuries, &amp; then there are the workers who have nothing, and live in very poor conditions. Calder and his family are workers, and make many sacrifices as Hector's people.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/79f266db-49cf-4229-a4b9-c9771d588ca3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418589070i/12842368._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 79f266db-49cf-4229-a4b9-c9771d588ca3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When Calder is around 10 yrs. old a beautiful little girl named Eden is brought to live at Acadia. They are all told she is the blessed one. Hector will make her his bride when she's 18, &amp; she will help lead them to the hereafter. She is like the princess of Acadia. Calder meets Eden as a child and their friendship grows through the years. Their friendship eventually turns into real feelings that neither know how to handle. Calder tries to remember Eden is off limits, and that he doesn't have to act on his attraction. Eden knows it's an impossible situation, but Calder was the most beautiful boy she'd ever seen. His beauty stole her breath. He was so kind and honorable, and her only friend. He gave her comfort, and made her feel special.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/9c40422c-6e94-4973-8293-62ca37d682af.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418589984i/12842555.jpg" alt=" photo 9c40422c-6e94-4973-8293-62ca37d682af.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even though they know nothing could ever happen between them, they can't fight the desire to be close to each other. They are helpless to stop their feelings from growing, &amp; no longer have control over their hearts.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/76382f5e-af5d-4736-ae7c-4208b3712ff9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418507533i/12812781.jpg" alt=" photo 76382f5e-af5d-4736-ae7c-4208b3712ff9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As they fall deeply in love, they begin to question their leader. They long for freedom, and to choose their own destiny in life. They have been obedient &amp; trusted Hector, but now they are questioning his ideas. They want a life together, and risk it all to make their dreams a reality.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/5df88151-b227-48d9-9a84-ca9739ae1d5c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418590759i/12842673.jpg" alt=" photo 5df88151-b227-48d9-9a84-ca9739ae1d5c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This poor couple has such a struggle throughout this book. Most of my GR friends loved this book. Although I loved this couple, it was just too much sad for one book for my tastes. I still thought the writing was fabulous &amp; love this author, but the whole cult topic wasn't for me. <br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/f1647087-57df-4fa4-8c40-7432d7ae8bdf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418505698i/12812599.jpg" alt=" photo f1647087-57df-4fa4-8c40-7432d7ae8bdf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-To me, he looked like a god who had come straight down from Elysium.<br><br>-And his smile...his smile lit up my world, even from afar. He was perfect.<br><br>-He still made my heart beat out of my own chest and his beauty mesmerized me, but now the desire to know who he really was filled my thoughts. <br><br>-My heart soared. I'd know that voice anywhere. I'd know that voice in the midst of a thousand clanging symbols, or in the deep darkness of a never-ending cave. It moved inside me.<br><br>-I want you to be mine, and only mine.<br><br>-This was wrong. But if it was, then why did it feel like I would die without it? Why did Eden's touch suddenly feel necessary to my very existence?<br><br>-I feel your lips on me, Eden. When I close my eyes, when I'm awake. I taste you. You are my first breath, and my last.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/Book%20ladies/Couples%20Pics/edb102b7-c0a9-4c73-94f0-00b50f75748b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419366807i/13046675._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo edb102b7-c0a9-4c73-94f0-00b50f75748b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-"Your mine, Eden. You always have been, from the very first second I saw you."<br><br>-Calder kissed me in a way that made me believe I had not only always been his, but I would be his forever.<br><br>-She was so beautiful, I felt something close to fear looking at her- like no matter what I did, no matter what I tried, I'd never get enough of her. I'd never resist her pull.<br><br>-She had every part of me. I was hers.<br><br>-I want you. I want all of you. And I want you to have all of me.<br><br>-"My heart is yours. My life is yours. My body is yours. My art, my dreams. You own each and every part of me."<br><br>-I trusted this man with everything in me. I trusted him with my body and my heart. I trusted him with my life. I felt precious, loved.</span>

<div id="review_1046693149" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1046693149" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1046693149?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23196814-becoming-calder">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1046693149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14661640518543780476"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413221530i/11480262._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"As long as we're both under the same moon, we'll always find a way to each other." <br/><br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>Wow. My feelings. My thoughts. This book was unlike anything I had ever read before. It was original and unforgettable and beautifully written. I cannot wait to read the next book.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413221530i/11480263._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am a big fan of Mia Sheridan. I love the fact that her stories are ones you can't forget and that her charact</span>
  <span id="freeText14661640518543780476" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413221530i/11480262._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"As long as we're both under the same moon, we'll always find a way to each other." <br><br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Wow. My feelings. My thoughts. This book was unlike anything I had ever read before. It was original and unforgettable and beautifully written. I cannot wait to read the next book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413221530i/11480263._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am a big fan of Mia Sheridan. I love the fact that her stories are ones you can't forget and that her characters are the same way. This book was just like that. I loved the story, although I though I might not at first. It took me a bit of time to get into and I thought this would be the first Mia Sheridan book I might have to step away from. The problem for me was the fact that this dealt with religion and that usually isn't my thing. But, I am so happy I kept going because it was an amazing story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“He was goodness-raw, unguarded goodness. It glowed in him. It was impossible to not want to drown in that type of beauty.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Acadia is a place where a religious community/cult reside. Calder has been living there his whole life. They are isolated from the "Big Community"(the rest of the world). They all work hard with very little to their name. All Calder has is his family and best friend Xander. The members of council, however, seem to have so much more. They have all the modern conveniences that the workers do not. Calder wants to be more than just a water bearer, he wants to be on council and learn more about the "Big Community. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401406928ra/9798958.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>'Calder kissed me in a way that made me believe I had not only always been his, but I would be his forever. In this life or any other. In his kiss was the promise that wherever he and I existed, we would belong to each other.'<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>One day, Hector--the leader--returns to Acadia because he has found his "Chosen One", just like the prophecy said he would. Hector brings in a little girl named Eden, who he plans to marry when she turns eighteen so she can lead them to "Elysium"/heaven. Calder, a boy himself, becomes interested in Eden, and Eden seems to feel the same way. They start a bit of a friendship but, Eden is forbidden so Calder stays away. Years go by, and they watch each other grow from children to young adults. The feelings of attraction grow, never diminishing with time. Soon, the inevitable happens, they bump into each other at a spring and continue to see each other there in secret. They eventually fall in love, but they are unsure of what do since Eden is betrothed to Hector. It seems all they can do is escape.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413222138ra/11480370.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I’m going to take you away from here, to a place where my bed is your bed, and my home is your home. And in that place, I’ll never be more than an arm’s reach from you.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>The story was told in alternating POV's. I loved that we get both because it was really beautiful to see them both fall in love with each other. They are each other's firsts, so my heart melted completely reading about them exploring one another. My heart felt for them and their situation. This is where I became completely captivated by the story. Hector suspects what is happening between them and becomes insane with trying to keep them apart. He will not allow anyone to disrupt the prophecy. I LOATHED Hector and his accomplice Clive. They were horrible. They were selfish and mean, which was a total contradiction to Hector's teachings. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413222138ra/11480371.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Calder, my heart is yours, as is my life, my body, my dreams. You own each and every part of me, in this lifetime and any other."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>My feelings were everywhere while reading this book. The angst of wondering if Calder and Eden would make it almost killed me. I got angry, scared, teared up, smiled so big, and swooned. There was that innocent quality in the relationship between Calder and Eden that had me hooked. I loved them both dearly as I did the secondary characters Maya and Xander. The writing was stunning. This ended with a big cliffhanger, so I am really happy that the next book is out. I can't wait to start it. Overall, I loved this incredible and unique story. I definitely recommend you give this a try.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413221530i/11480263._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14661640518543780476" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1073820337" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1073820337" />
    <a title="Hildy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5033175-hildy"><img alt="Hildy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474498190p2/5033175.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1073820337?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hildy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hildy" href="/user/show/5033175-hildy">Hildy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1073820337" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4391203464202677482">Am I broken?<br/><br/>No, seriously. This is becoming a huge pattern. It goes something like this:<br/><br/>A new book is released (usually self-published).<br/>Every review is 5 stars and even 6+++ stars. *eyeroll*<br/>I fall for the hype and go and buy it.<br/>I read it.<br/>I sit there completely baffled, wondering if I've read the same book as everyone else.<br/>I write a review and look like a huge cranky-ass.<br/>I hit publish and hope that I don't piss someone off.<br/><br/><br/>Let me rewind a bit. I downloaded this book and was about to start. Then I</span>
  <span id="freeText4391203464202677482" style="display:none">Am I broken?<br /><br />No, seriously. This is becoming a huge pattern. It goes something like this:<br /><br />A new book is released (usually self-published).<br />Every review is 5 stars and even 6+++ stars. *eyeroll*<br />I fall for the hype and go and buy it.<br />I read it.<br />I sit there completely baffled, wondering if I've read the same book as everyone else.<br />I write a review and look like a huge cranky-ass.<br />I hit publish and hope that I don't piss someone off.<br /><br /><br />Let me rewind a bit. I downloaded this book and was about to start. Then I did a double-take at the cute guy on the cover. Were those nipples...and a SCARF? Why hadn't I noticed that before? WTH, people? I had to text JJ and tell her that I was going to rename the book Man Nipples and Pashminas (because I find myself amusing sometimes). So, I put the book away because I had to shake my snarky attitude and give this a fair chance. My friend Mandy loved this and we often have similar tastes in books, so I needed to shake it off. Once I started, the explanation for the image was given quite early, but I still wasn't buying it.<br /><br />Enough about the cover.<br /><br />The first 40% of the book was a bit slow. It wasn't completely boring, it just wasn't drawing me in to stay with it. It was okay. I didn't really love the overall plot that was driven by a religious cult, but it didn't turn me off completely either. I guess I was just waiting for this amazing writing that I kept hearing about. The thing is, Mia Sheridan is not a bad writer at all. I just think she falls into the trap that a lot of New Adult writers fall into and that is...excessive cheese. Let me give an example:<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>As long as we're both under the same moon, we'll always find each other.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I thought I was reading An American Tail for a second there.<br /><br />And what about the fact that "morning glory" is used 57 times in the book, most often as a term of endearment? 57 TIMES!!!<br /><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Eden, Eden, oh Eden, my love, my morning glory.</i>
</blockquote><br />What's the matter with me that I don't think this is swoony? Women all over Goodreads are passing out from the these romantic moments and I'm thinking, "Huh?" I don't butterflyingly love this kind of stuff. &lt;---See what I did there? That's another one that I couldn't choke down. I mean, I read romance because I fall pretty hard for the romantic moments in books, but they also have to have some believability. Perhaps my husband has ruined things. I get a kiss and a "You're still hot." every once in a while but that's pretty much all as far as swoony dialogue. :) Let's blame Big B.<br /><br />I was really close to giving this 3 stars because it did have moments that held my interest. I did think the main characters were sweet, even though they were 17 and 18. They did have some pretty hawt sexy times. But, but... I just can't. This just doesn't stand out to me as either an amazing story or amazing writing. The last part got pretty exciting but I feel a little disappointed that I have to buy another book to see how the story ends. Do I want to know? Yeah. Do I care enough to buy it? Nope. I may pick it up if it ever goes on sale and see what happens. Then again, I may not.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4391203464202677482" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText4392538639048540466" style="display:none">This had me heart broken <br><br><a href="http://i.imgur.com/avT8rvx" title="" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1072339299" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1072339299" />
    <a title="Ilze" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12206696-ilze"><img alt="Ilze" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1355328800p2/12206696.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1072339299?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ilze" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ilze" href="/user/show/12206696-ilze">Ilze</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23196814-becoming-calder">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12206696-ilze?shelf=heart-wrenching">heart-wrenching</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12206696-ilze?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12206696-ilze?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12206696-ilze?shelf=2014-release">2014-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12206696-ilze?shelf=ultimate-book-boyfriend">ultimate-book-boyfriend</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1072339299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8449671709295239888">If you are looking for a unique, exceptionally well written book with different setting and great story line - you SHOULD give this a try!<br/><br/><b>"Where do you find your strength, Morning Glory?" She gave me a small smile in return.<br/>"From you," she whispered...</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412706845i/11410927.jpg' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Calder and Eden, both live in a place which is cut out of the real world. Religious cult with its own laws and order. Calder is one of the workers, who have to work everyday to provide for the community. Eden is the blessed one who is meant to marr</span>
  <span id="freeText8449671709295239888" style="display:none">If you are looking for a unique, exceptionally well written book with different setting and great story line - you SHOULD give this a try!<br><br><b>"Where do you find your strength, Morning Glory?" She gave me a small smile in return.<br>"From you," she whispered...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412706845i/11410927.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Calder and Eden, both live in a place which is cut out of the real world. Religious cult with its own laws and order. Calder is one of the workers, who have to work everyday to provide for the community. Eden is the blessed one who is meant to marry the head of the cult when she reaches 18 years of age. They both have learned about sins and what they can and can't do in the place they live. Despite of that they couldn't stay away from each other since the day their eyes met. A forbidden love story of two young people with aren't afraid to dream and want more from the world than what they are given. <br><br><b>"No one should ever stop you from gaining knowledge if you want it."</b><br><br>Becoming Calder was both refreshing and frustrating read. Overall, I really liked it and the first part of the book was pure joy, but the problem for me started when the main characters were stuck in the place they didn't want to be, but weren't willing to leave yet. I understand their reasons for waiting to leave, but in the end the reasons were pointless and caused more suffering than was necessary. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412706845i/11410928._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"So, speaking of squash, our lesson today is going to be on the stars."<br>I raised an eyebrow. "What does squash have to do with the stars?"<br>"Oh, you've never heard of the constellation, Squasharius?"</b><br><br>Eden and Calder were absolutely adorable! Their love, although forbidden was so sweet and pure. I loved both of them (Calder 100x more) and the cutest they were when Eden was daydreaming about Calder's body and Calder thinking about coca-cola ♥ However, I constantly had to remind myself that they are kids and they don't know much of life, because so many things could have been avoided if they acted smarter.<br><br>Also, I absolutely loved Maya and Xander and their interactions with Calder. I think they both were such a huge part of the story, because they showed us how wonderful and honorable Calder is ♥<br><br>Anyway, they all were just so cute that the first part of the book I was like this<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412706845ra/11410929.gif" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Despite of the lovable characters I had a few problems with this book. <br>One of the things was the religious cult setting which I don't mind, but it is always kind of tricky for me to get into it. I kind of understand the people and their decisions in the cult, but I can't help myself and think of them as idiots. My problem here was that the religious cult took such a huge part of the book and it was crazy like movie 'Drive Angry' crazy. <br><br>Also, with forbidden love stories there is always that moment where you know that their love is going to be discovered. And here I was constantly waiting for that moment and waiting and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[then waiting for them to be properly punished. I think I would have been more surprised if Clive had not find them in the city.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br> <br>I know most of people aren't bothered by either of the two things I mentioned above, so don't let it stop you from reading this. <br><br><b>"If this is the last piece of heaven I get before I'm dragged down to hell, then I'll gladly take it."</b><br><br>Lastly, I really enjoyed this book, even if it made me so angry that I wanted to commit bloody murder (kill Hector). It was another great story by talented Mia Sheridan and you know it is a wonderful book when you have pages and pages of highlights on your kindle ♥<br><br>Thanks to all the BR lovely ladies ♥<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8449671709295239888" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1107091532" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1107091532" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1107091532?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23196814-becoming-calder">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1107091532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6906187494090814374">3.5 - 4 ★'s <br/><br/>Becoming Calder is basically a story of two young children being drawn to each other and eventually falling in love. Is it allowed? No, it's not and therein lies the problem. <br/><br/>I have to admit that I was a bit thrown off by the subject matter of this book that I read in my friend's reviews. It doesn't mentioned it in the blurb but in case you don't know and want to: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[they're in a religious cult. <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416363486i/11943681._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And I didn't like some of the things involving that subject m</span>
  <span id="freeText6906187494090814374" style="display:none">3.5 - 4 ★'s <br><br>Becoming Calder is basically a story of two young children being drawn to each other and eventually falling in love. Is it allowed? No, it's not and therein lies the problem. <br><br>I have to admit that I was a bit thrown off by the subject matter of this book that I read in my friend's reviews. It doesn't mentioned it in the blurb but in case you don't know and want to: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they're in a religious cult. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416363486i/11943681._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I didn't like some of the things involving that subject matter. But it is what Calder and Eden struggle with...good and bad, love and hate, doing what you're told and doing what is right. <br><br>You can't help but adore Calder...he is such a good person and he wants to do the right thing. He stays away from Eden for a very long time but things change as he gets older and when he becomes disillusioned...aka wiser. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416359793i/11943396.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eden, well, yes...she is good too but first and foremost, she wants what she wants. She doesn't want to do what she's told to do. There is definitely a fire inside her and that does aid her in many ways. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416362145i/11943588._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Eden and Calder together. Their nicknames are so sweet and just how fascinated they are with each other. I loved their secret meeting place! It was wonderful reading about them falling in love but really sad at the same time because of all the obstacles. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416363486i/11943680._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to give a shout out to Xander. He grew up with Calder and eventually becomes friends with Eden as well. I love the relationship between him and Calder...they are <b>
  <i>brothers.</i>
</b> <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Whatever I have—" <br><br>"—you have half."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>So the drama...well, if you read my spoiler then you can just imagine what happens. It was kind of hard to read what happened to all three of them, Calder, Eden and Xander. <br><br>The ending wraps right back around to the prologue so at least that finally makes sense. And we kind of get to find out what happens to Calder. <b>But</b>...it does leave you hanging. I would really recommend if you're going to read this book that you have <i>Finding Eden</i> ready to go. You're going to want to find out what happens. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416362467i/11943615.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "Where do you find your strength, Morning Glory?" <br><br>♥ "I've wanted you for so long. So long. Every waking minute, in my dreams, too. I want to bury myself in you, <i>drown</i> in you, and never come up for air. I want you to be mine, and <i>only</i> mine."<br> <br>♥ "My heart is yours. My life is yours. My body is yours. My art, my dreams. You own each and every part of me."<br><br>♥ "I love you, Morning Glory." <br><br>"I love you, too, Butterscotch."<br> <br>♥ "I'll never, ever forget my first shower," Calder whispered.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer889440592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12148488770292952196"><b>3 STARS</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412633546i/11399458._SY540_.jpg' alt='' height='430' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Genre:</b> Young forbidden romance – based in a remote Cult community.<br/><b>Cover:</b> 7/10<br/><b>Writing:</b> 8/10<br/><b>Heroine:</b> 7/10<br/><b>Hero:</b> 8/10<br/><b>Humour:</b> 0/10<br/><b>Hotness:</b> 2/10<br/><b>Romance:</b> 10/10<br/><b>Extra book Details:</b> Heroine & Hero POV; 1st person. Book 1 of 2. Approx 338 Kindle pages.<br/><br/>Cult leader Hector discovers his blessed one at her tender age of six, but so does water bearer Calder.<br/><br/>A forbidden relationship grows between Eden and Calder. But Eden is betrothed to Hector and Calder has no power.<br/><br/>Soon, it will all come crashing down.</span>
  <span id="freeText12148488770292952196" style="display:none"><b>3 STARS</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412633546i/11399458._SY540_.jpg" alt="" height="430" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Genre:</b> Young forbidden romance – based in a remote Cult community.<br><b>Cover:</b> 7/10<br><b>Writing:</b> 8/10<br><b>Heroine:</b> 7/10<br><b>Hero:</b> 8/10<br><b>Humour:</b> 0/10<br><b>Hotness:</b> 2/10<br><b>Romance:</b> 10/10<br><b>Extra book Details:</b> Heroine &amp; Hero POV; 1st person. Book 1 of 2. Approx 338 Kindle pages.<br><br>Cult leader Hector discovers his blessed one at her tender age of six, but so does water bearer Calder.<br><br>A forbidden relationship grows between Eden and Calder. But Eden is betrothed to Hector and Calder has no power.<br><br>Soon, it will all come crashing down.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”If I have to live in Elysium for eternity with someone I don't love, I thought that maybe a kiss from you, even just one, would make it bearable.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407594236i/10744003.jpg" alt="" height="20" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here I go, in the minority again...<br><br>I went into this book blind, so to find out that the whole thing is based in a Cult, was kind of weird for me. The whole brainwash/mass death thing was kind of yucky for me too. It almost felt like an historical read because of the dialogue and lack of contemporary thought from the characters and surroundings.<br><br>The first half of the book involved a lot of bonding between the two forbidden lovers, there's a hellva lot of romance which was a little overboard for my tastes. It also included plenty of information on how this Cult community worked.<br><br>The second half was a better half for me; the drama spiked. But I felt more disturbed when it came towards the end.<br><br>I did like the forbidden aspect, the whole Princess Jasmine/Aladdin/Jafar relationship, Calders bestie and the water theme. The setting was unique, I thought Calder was very brave and admirable, but the very romanticized dialogue, the dull-ish first half and the disturbing setting put me off.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407252752i/10663054.jpg" alt="" height="110" width="210" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12148488770292952196" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bC1Hl95vsiL8KKp3a/ucuLRWbiZAPY1aAD/ezI1K+rO2bsZtzVgPQRJQuLoht0CkJfDbUwWA+Kpy0s/hMl5ttQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LnI1Qx2Kf9k8vMlDIwajHUjqPrTCl6NwjW+730E4Gc/0MbS5Dr3CutLE245pSn8B2UyLwYcq1oD/gqry/iyOyQ==')})
  }

Circumstances leave her stranded in an unfamiliar city, and in an embarrassing moment of weakness, she meets a guarded young man with a past he’d do anything to change...\n\nBeckett Copeland spent two years in prison for armed robbery, and is now struggling to keep his head above water. A bike messenger by day, he speeds around New York City, riding fast and hard but going nowhere, his criminal record holding him back almost as much as the guilt of his crime. \n\nZelda and Beckett form a grudging alliance of survival, and in between their stubborn clash of wills, they slowly begin to provide each other with the warmth of forgiveness, healing, and maybe even love. But when Zelda and Beckett come face to face with their pasts, they must choose to hold on to the guilt and regret that bind them, or let go and open their hearts for a shot at happiness. \n\nThe Butterfly Project is a novel that reveals the power of forgiveness, and how even the smallest decisions of the heart can—like the flutter of a butterfly’s wings—create currents that strengthen into gale winds, altering the course of a life forever. \n\n#standalone<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"10926143680412779327\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n
